The horn flute to use at Ragnarok that only Hayes possessed, the Origin Variety.

Previously, when Poseidon was resurrected, Hayes was hiding inside the shadow of her robe and he couldn't see what she was doing.

But, two days ago when Hayes showed up in front of him, the horn flute that he saw she was holding had strange pattern engraved on it.

"Is that, everything you want to say?"

"No, putting aside my advice, I have one thing I want to ask. Assuming that what I said was all true‐do you really have the intention to save that childhood friend of yours?"

"…………"

In respond to Fugil's question, Lux met his gaze wordlessly.

"As I thought, you haven't changed huh. You are still the same like that time, foolish and weak."

Fugil sighed in exasperation and he looked up to empty air.

With his back still facing the deep ultramarine of the darkness, he formed a smile that could even be called as evil countenance.

"Don't you notice that you too are trying to do the same thing like that woman called Relie? Saving what is important, an existence that is irreplaceable for you. Certainly it sounds nice, but in actuality doing that is a betrayal toward this country and those students. You are committing a folly that might turn you into the enemy of the world."

"It's evil‐is that what you want to say?"

"No……"

Unexpectedly Fugil instantly denied it.

"It's troubling because it's not evil or anything. However, if there are a thousand people then there will be a thousand path of justice‐I don't have any intention to speak any tomfoolery like that. They don't have any awareness of good and evil, this is nothing more than them merely in conflict regarding something that they cannot concede, as only natural."

Fugil continued so still wearing his composed smile.

"That is the nature of living thing as it were. People who have been hungry in the past will try to gather more food. The weak will try to obtain even stronger power. People who have their important person robbed from them will try to protect their important person desperately. And then‐"

Fugil peered into the eyes of Lux who was still holding up his sword and laughed.

"Someone who wasn't loved by anyone, will try to be loved ny anyone."

"…………"

Lux didn't reply at all toward Fugil's words.

But, he narrowed his shadowed eyes and spoke.

"Why, did you kill all the imperial family and army of the old empire that day? Your true objective‐what is it?"

"The current you won't understand even if I told you."

Fugil replied with a tone that was mixed with a sigh.

"But, someday you will understand if you keep walking your path as it is.

In the future each nation will develop even more intense conflict. The lot of the new kingdom will approach to make use of your and your comrade's strength. They will come to take you into their fold. They will try to lure you into a repulsive path, carrying the great cause that is no other than'to protect the new kingdom's peace'."

"…………"

"You should understand before long. Just what did I do at that day. Why did I make use of you. If you get involved with this country again, and yet you will still try to persist in your ideal, then‐"

Fugil turned around. He tilted his head and looked back with a smile.

"You will understand that nothing exist in this world. Whether it's your ideal, or what you want to protect, everything."

He left behind only those words and walked away.

When Lux stepped forward to chase after him, he saw Fugil drew out his Sword Device.

The blade glistened with light, silver lines were running through it.

The sword emitted undulating faint light of seven colors.

"Uu……, ku……!"

Sharp and piercing pain instantly ran at the back of Lux's eyes. Lux pressed his hand on his forehead and fell on one knee.

When he noticed, Fugil was vanishing like a mist.

It was as though nothing was there right from the start.

"Oooii! Lux!"

A voice came while Lux was staring at the darkness in blank amazement.

When he turned around, he saw the figure of Lisha approaching him in a

run.

"Lisha, sama……"

"I finally completed it! I succeeded in the last system removal so that your Bahamut can use the awakened state! It's thanks to the code that your little sister solved. But‐"

She talked in excitement until midway before her tone became faltering.

"This thing, as I thought it's better not to use it……. It's a good thing that the ability can come to light but, the burden is too great. Using that with

Bahamut is still‐"

"Please teach me! I beg you!"

"Wah!?"

Lux took both her hands and pleaded.

The surprised Lisha was blushing while,

"Ca, calm down. Certainly it's a failed work right now, but perhaps it will become usable depending on the future improvement. That's why, don't be reckless. Letting you do something dangerous by yourself more than this is‐"

"I beg you, Lisha-sama."

Lux sent her a serious gaze and didn't let go of her hands.

"A time will come where I have to use it. At this rate, it might turn into something I regret again. I‐don't want, to repeat the same thing like that time!"

"That, time……?"

When Lisha tilted her head, a strange scene was revived at the back of Lux's mind.

That day when the old empire was finished.

Sparks danced in the sky, swarms of Drag-Ride crossed in the dark night.

And then‐.

"-……!?"

The consciousness of Lux that was receding away was called back.

The sensation of soft and smooth small hands.

In front of him Lisha was grasping back at Lux's hands while her cheeks were slightly dyed red.

"I, I get it."

She directed her gaze at Lux with slightly exasperated face and puffed up cheeks.

"You won't listen to anything once you already speak. Even though normally you are that humble……. But, the code to release Bahamut is complicated, so I have to teach you from scratch you know?"

"Thank you very much, Lisha-sama."

"……Fuh"

Seeing Lux bowing his head really deeply, Lisha smiled with a troubled look.

With this, the preparation was in order.

This was the only plan left that could save Philuffy within tonight.

Lux resolved himself like that in his heart. It was then Lisha suddenly lifted up her face,

"Come to think of it, where is Relie? I was looking for her since some time ago to get the permission to use the awakened mode‐" "‐"

Lux suddenly realized hearing that.

"……I'm sorry, Lisha-sama."

And then a few second later Lux turned to face Lisha and told her with a serious expression.

"Can I ask you to contact everyone? If Relie-san cannot be found anywhere then‐"

Saying that, Lux resolved himself.

It was the determination to plunge himself into the upheaval once more.

"I'll look for her. At the deepest level of the Ruin‐"

Part 3

Ten minutes later. Everyone split to search for Relie at the likely places like the boarding house, the practice ground, and other places.

But, there wasn't any sign of her at all.

There was also the possibility that she was kidnapped by someone, but Lux had an idea about her whereabouts.

The Ruin.

In order to look for a way to erase the Ratatoskr of the Ragnarok taking hold of Philuffy, Relie planned to slip into the deepest level.

Therefore, Lux would slip into the ruin alone in order to not involve the other students.

From here onward, there was the possibility that the students would get dragged into a serious crime.

If they weren't careful, it wouldn't end as only the problem of the new kingdom. It might become a big international problem that could affect the international tournament that would start after this.

(But……, I cannot leave her alone like this.)

At the night duty room in the boardinghouse where Relie was.

There was a letter placed on the table there. It was only written with 'please take care of Philuffy'.

Lux who sensed an alarming atmosphere from the letter hurriedly moved to exit the boardinghouse, it was then‐.

"Lu-chan. Wait."

"Philuffy……!?"

When he looked there, Philuffy was getting up with her face red and her body staggering.

"You must not! Right now, if you don't sleep‐"

There was no way he could talk about the Ragnarok, so Lux told her like that in panic.

However,

"I, already know."

"Eh……?"

"That in my body, there is Abyss."

Philuffy said that with her usual absentminded tone and serious face.

The moment Lux heard that, the inside of his head became blank.

"Philuf, fy……"

A listless voice was squeezed out from Lux's lungs.

"Sorry, for staying quiet."

Philuffy calmly smiled while saying that.

"……I noticed it recently but, well, it doesn't really matter."

"Eeh!?"

Lux was taken by surprise from Philuffy's words that were still at her own pace even now.

But,

"Yes. because, it's important that I live. Because, if I die, both Onee-chan and Lu-chan will surely be sad."

Philuffy lightly put her hand on her chest and muttered.

"Onee-chan, after Okaa-san died from sickness, she looked like she was really lonely. That was why, I thought, I cannot die."

Philuffy continued talking while smiling. Her tone was detached in nostalgia.

"Lu-chan is also someone who get lonely really easily, so I thought that it will be really painful for you, if I die."

"‐"

"That's why‐I'm glad, I'm alive until today."

Lux's chest tightened hearing that sentence that was like a surprise attack.

He wondered since when he misunderstood that Philuffy didn't notice.

Normally Philuffy was silent and she wasn't good in expressing her emotion, but with her sharp intuition, she understood about Lux and Relie more than anyone.

Of course that included how Lux and Relie were actually alive while carrying unbearable loneliness and wound.

And also how if Philuffy who was their support died, both of them would lose sight of themselves.

Philuffy knew all about the change of her own body, she noticed it, but she still tried to live.

"But, it's already okay."

Saying that, Philuffy made a transient smile.

"Because, Lu-chan already made, a lot of important people. Because, you've become strong."

She said that with a voice that sounded just a little lonely.

"That's why surely, you'll be fine."

That voice that was trying to reassure him was the same like that time seven years ago.

However, it was different from that time.

"You're wrong-!"

Lux reflexively yelled, but he couldn't speak further.

And then, he strongly embraced the body of Philuffy before him.

"Lu, chan?"

Warm body and the faint sweet fragrance.

Lux whispered while pushing down his emotion that usually made his heart pounded hard at this kind of time.

"I'm, no good……. I haven't changed at all since then……I'm still, weaker than anyone else!"

Faint surprise and perplexity could be felt from the girl inside his arms. Even so, Lux didn't let go of her.

"Don't disappear……. The wound inside me still remained all this time since that day! It was because Philuffy saved me that day, because you stayed alive until today, that I could fight as the prince of Arcadia Empire!" A person who lost the important person that they ought to protect.

A person who cursed the whole world and turned it into enemy, such

person wouldn't be able to change a country.

"That's why, don't go! Don't disappear! I absolutely, this time for sure I absolutely will save you! That's why‐"

"I see."

A gentle sensation of a hand caressed Lux's front hair.

When he noticed, Philuffy was making a faint smile at him.

"Lu-chan, still haven't changed."

"…………"

Philiffy caressed Lux's cheek in nostalgia and muttered.

"Thank you. I'll wait."

It was only a brief sentence.

It was the demonstration of will showed by the silent Philuffy using words.

Lux understood everything just from that.

"Please, take care of Onee-chan."

"Yes."

Lux nodded firmly and turned around.

And then, the moment he turned his back, Philuffy's voice called out to him.

"Also, call me Phi-chan, okay?"

"Yes……sorry."

Lux smiled wryly hearing Philuffy's words that sounded a bit sullen. "……Then, I'm going, Phi-chan."

And then Lux exited the boarding house and started running.

Part 4

Lux ran at full speed along the coast late at night.

Lux asked Lisha and others to communicate to everyone at the surface to not go near the Ruin, and for them to wait until Relie and Lux returned.

If he tried to get the cooperation of Lisha and others, they would get dragged into this dangerous battle where there would be no return.

Lux jumped on the deck of the Ark, opened the door of the direct passage, then stepped above the relay portal.

"Come, the symbol of power the winged dragon of crest. Obey my sword and take flight, Wyvern"

First Lux equipped Wyvern and waited. Then the transfer began.

The corridor of the eighth floor that they previously reached now had bluish white lamp shining, different from before.

"Did the system, recover?"

La Cruche was recovering her memory at the control room area and restored her authority as the Gear Leader.

Originally everything should turn out well with that but‐.

"GURORORO……!"

A weird growl came from behind an object.

"Don't tell me‐!?"

When Lux noticed, the thing already leaped at him.

"SHAAaAAAAH!"

A winged person made from a solid material attacked while letting out a piercing cry.

Lux barely used his sword as shield and blocked the first attack.

"Gargoyle!? Why here……!"

The Automaton(La Cruche) said that Abyss mostly shouldn't appear at eighth floor and below. It was because originally it wasn't a place that should be protected.

For that reason Relie hurried ahead thinking that she could reach until the deepest level even without Drag-Ride but‐.

(No, right now isn't the time to think about that!)

Lux instantly erased his various imagination and poured his concentration to the battle in front of him.

He destroyed the second attack toward his Wyvern with the Scale Blade's Critical Hit.

"GUGAH, AAaAAH!"

The Gargoyle writhed when its sharp claw along with its right arm was pulverized.

But at the same time, even more enemy presence appeared as though they heard the scream.

There was a Chimera that he once witnessed together with Celis, a winged beast Gryphon, and also squid type Abyss called Kraken.

There were more than ten enemies just from what he could see.

The Abysses were taking formation that surrounded him in this place where there was little cover.

(This is bad, at this rate‐)

Although Lux was used to fight Abyss, this situation was still overwhelmingly disadvantageous for him.

He could face them down if he switched his Drag-Ride into Bahamut!

"SHAaAAAAH!"

The Gargoyle roared and it was about to attack Lux once more, it was then‐.

*DOON!*

Dazzling flash ran through empty air and hit the Gargoyle.

"GA, aAAAAH!"

Its dying scream was drowned by an explosive sound. It scattered black fragments and vanished.

The canon attack that was fired from behind Lux pierced the one armed Gargoyle.

"As always, you are a forceful guy huh."

"Eh?"

Lux's eyes opened wide in surprise and he turned his gaze to the surrounding.

At that time, large type Abysses that were waiting for the chance to attack had their body frozen one after another.

"I understand that you're feeling impatient, but it's putting the car before the horse if you're defeated."

When Lux turned toward the voice from behind him, he found the figure of Lisha and Krulcifer there wearing Tiamat and Fafnir.

Without even any time to let out any word in surprise, lightning ran at the surrounding and turned the frozen Abysses into ash one after another.

"The headmaster is like that, but you too are also really rash. I conclude that a lecture is needed when we get back."

Celis who was wearing the Divine Drag-Ride of lightning Lindwurm told Lux that in exasperation.

"It appears that the headmaster is going ahead until the tenth floor. From the reaction, La Cruche is also beside her. Abysses are approaching them from the surrounding. It's better to hurry if you want to chase them."

Noct said from behind while confirming with her Drake's radar.

"Aah but, a lot of enemies are coming down to this area, so Lux-chi , you can just leave this to us! Ah, you can pay us back for this later on!"

"Well, putting aside Tillfur, those three Divine Drag-Ride users are really something, so leave this place to us lad."

"Uwah, meanie! Even though I'm enduring my fear like this!"

Hearing Sharis's words, Tillfur showed her actual feeling and acted flustered.

It seemed that everyone gathered here because they noticed Lux's objective.

However,

"Why is everyone, doing this‐"

"I told everyone."

*step*, A small walking sound echoed and a small statured girl walked forward.

The girl wearing school uniform was Airi.

"I accidentally listened to Nii-san and headmaster's talk. After hearing that, it's simple to predict how Nii-san will act so‐"

Saying that, Airi looked up toward Lux with slightly anxious face.

"Nii-san is going to save Philuffy-san right? No matter what."

"……Yes."

"Then, let's start. Doing it with everyone should have higher chance of success. Surely‐"

"Airi, please be careful. It's enemy reinforcement."

Noct raised a tensed voice, at the same time everyone stood ready.

"Lux. Go quickly! We will take care of these guys!"

Right after Lisha raised her voice, Krulcifer also sent a dragon voice that was transmitted to only Lux.

'We're going to catch up soon. I think that my authentication might be necessary to open the door to the deepest level. For now, go on ahead to the headmaster‐'

"Yes!"

Lux replied while flying his Wyvern at the same time.

"Everyone, thank you."

Lux said his thanks to everyone who gathered here and rushed through the passage in full speed.

Lux thought while going straight through the remaining floors in high speed.

Even though he intended to not involve them, in the end he made them to fuss about him needlessly instead.

Even though there should be no time for them to hear about the detail from Airi, even so everyone rushed to help him.

He felt a mysterious feeling.

The thing that he couldn't obtain all this time since that day when he was a child.

Perhaps this time for sure he would obtain irreplaceable comrades that he could trust.

And then, even now Lux was scared that those comrades would abandon him, or perhaps he would lose them because of his fault.

That was something that didn't change since that day where he harbored doubt toward the old empire(that country). (But‐!)

There was already no time for hesitation.

The time of his childhood where he couldn't do anything.

And then, the day of revolution five years ago when he was betrayed and failed.

His current answer would come out after this.

Passing through the scenery that was flowing in high speed over him, Lux resolved himself, at that moment,

"Relie-san!" He saw it.

"……Lux-kun-!?"

He overtook Relie who was together with La Cruche and intercepted the beast type Abyss that was standing in their way.

"Uo, OaaAAAAH!"

The Abyss that was called as Werewolf received the Critical Hit from the Scale Blade and its upper body was blown away.

After confirming the Abyss's death, Lux walked toward Relie who was falling on her knees.

"Are you all right? Is anywhere hurt‐?"

"How, did you know I came here‐? No, rather than that……even you"

Relie opened her eyes in blank amazement while whispering.

"Yes. I'll also save Philuffy. No matter what, for sure."

"Is that so……"

Relie made a frail smile hearing Lux's words and she averted her gaze.

"……But, something like that, actually might not exist. Something like a way to save that girl, actually it's nowhere to be……. Even so‐I"

A voice that was filled with emptiness was squeezed out from Relie's lungs.

She used every way available in order to save her beloved little sister, then she realized that everything she did was for naught,

Even so, she couldn't give up.

Inside those words, there was the suffering of someone who continued to fight loneliness.

"It will be fine. Surely, we will manage somehow."

"…………"

Even so, Lux didn't take back the hand he offered and formed his words strongly.

"Besides I promised her, that this time for sure, I'll absolutely save her‐"

Relie looked down hearing Lux's voice that was filled with conviction.

But, this time she took Lux's hand and stood up.

"I'm sorry for dragging you into this. ‐But, thank you."

Relie wiped her eyes that were blotted with tears and silently stood up.

"Sorry to keep you waiting. Let's hurry."

Relie tensed her expression and turned her gaze toward her side. There La Cruche was smiling.

"I read the mood and stayed quiet. I'm a good child."

"Ah, isn't that right……"

Lux responded with a wry smile.

While no more Abyss came, they went down until the deepest level of eleventh floor. It was then Lisha and others caught up from behind.

"Master. Please touch the crest of the door and think silently. The door of the deepest part will open after that."

"I understand."

Krulcifer took a deep breath, then she walked toward the huge door.

At that time Lux whispered into the ear of Airi who was standing beside him.

"Airi, do you bring the horn flute?"

"Yes. I'm carrying it close to my person though‐"

"Then I have a request. If the situation become like what I predicted, I want you to use it."

When Lux began telling Airi about 'that plan' , Krulcifer's hand was held out toward the door.

The moment her hand touched, several streak of blue lightning ran on the surface of the door.

"-……!?"

Krulcifer leaked out a small moan from feeling a stimulus that felt like pain. Shining countless letters were emerging on the smooth surface of the door and it was opening.

'The authentication of Xfer is confirmed……connection complete. There is also no problem with the usage restriction. Unlocking is possible with mind control operation.'

The inorganic artificial voice could be heard. Bewilderment appeared on Relie's face.

"What happened? Krulcifer-san, you are……!?"

"I'll explain later. If we are still safe at that time‐"

Krulcifer closed her eyes with her hand still on the door and she concentrated.

And then the door rumbled and a strange vibration was transmitted through her hand, after that,

*GASHIiiIIIN!*

The door opened to four directions like flower petals along with heavy metallic sound.

An unimaginable sight was spreading there.

"Is this……the deepest level!?"

It was a vast dome shaped space that was surrounded with hard metallic wall.

That place which was illuminated by light source overhead looked like the colosseum of the ancient era.

"……Is this place really the deepest level, La Cruche?"

Celis's question was only natural.

Their image regarding the Ruin's deepest level was a huge treasure warehouse.

And yet, don't mention ancient text or tool of ancient era, not even a part of Drag-Ride could be found here.

When they had walked until nearly the center of the space, Relie watched the back of La Cruche with an expression that was a mix of bewilderment and anxiety.

"Is there some kind of mistake? Could it be, that your memory restoration faile‐?"

"That's not true."

La Cruche walked ahead. She then twirled around that caused her dress to flutter before answering.

Her height only reached until Lux's waist. She was a lovely girl that looked like little girl.

He didn't notice until now how the look of her eyes was covered with dark shadow.

"My memory restoration was a success. I remember everything. The thing that I should do is‐"

La Cruche smiled and lifted her hand.

It was the smile of a predator that caught its prey into a trap.

"getting rid of all of you, leaving not a single one alive."

A shudder ran through Lux and everyone else. In that instant, the thick door behind them closed swiftly.

"Wha-……!?"

When everyone turned around, it was already too late.

The thick last door was firmly closed. In front of it there were the silhouettes of two figures wearing black robe.

"What are you doing? Listen to what I'm saying as the supervisor‐"

When Lucifer was questioning her in panic, La Cruche bowed courteously.

"Master. I have the obligation to listen to your order. But that is not the top priority of the current me. As the Gear Leader of the Ark, I have to eliminate all of you, a family of the rebel who betrayed and overthrew my masters then invaded this place, and his comrades‐"

La Cruche glared at Lux with naked animosity filling her gaze.

Several scenes were resurrected at Lux's mind seeing that gaze.

The inside of the ship that was destroyed and fell into ruin that they saw right after entering the Ruin.

And then, the Ragnarok that appeared from the Ruin, Poseidon.

Fresh traces of destruction that weren't from the war of ancient era, which appeared to come from the invasion of the old empire ten-odd years ago.

Did La Cruche traced back that memory, and because of that she considered Lux who had the same features as her opponent? (But‐a family of the rebel……she said, what does she mean? Is there someone else other than me and the imperial family?)

He didn't understand.

Lux had no way of knowing about the truth of the old empire that had continued for several hundred years.

But, the footsteps of two people approaching from behind pulled Lux back into reality.

What existed ahead of his gaze when he turned around were two figures clad in robe.

The figure walking at the front pulled off her hood and showed her face.

It was a girl with shining silver hair and asymmetrically colored eyes‐Hayes.

"The negotiation breakdown huh, prince. No, you were moving like an idiot and carried out my objective just like I planned, so perhaps I ought to say thanks to you instead?" "You‐!?"

Lux who confirmed her identity muttered with a groan.

Why did the girl who told him to open the door at the afternoon was here?

She specified the time period and told him that he had to follow it was a trap.

Although he was threatened, Lux and others should have resistance of being made to open the last door just as Hayes ordered.

"You will regret it if you get cocky and talk too much you know? When you lose that is."

"You guys already lost by the time you came here and fell into my plan!

But, do your best to fight back! And then become food for Yggdrasil!"

The giant tree began to move once more along with the declaration.

Lisha and others also desperately fought back, but their every single move was surpassed.

And then‐, finally Tiamat's armor was dispelled because of excessive damage.

"U, aa……!"

"Lisha-sama-!?"

He held her body and retreated to the rear.

"Lisha-sama. Please let me use it. The other power hidden inside

Bahamut‐"

"…………"

That day five years ago‐.

The last day when the old kingdom perished and the palace fell.

Was Lisha also thinking back about that too?

Saying that, Lisha pulled out two Sword Devices.

"I promise."

Right after telling her that, Lux stood in front of Yggdrasil's way.

The remaining members were already wounded all over, they couldn't even fight.

"Now, you've resolved yourself right, false prince."

Hayes displayed a wicked smile. At that moment, dark red branches approached with speed several times faster than before.

But, from an inescapable situation, Lux's Bahamut cut the branches with speed that surpassed it.

One of the three hidden techniques, Quick Draw.

Lux let out a single flash with certainty, but against this powerful monster as the opponent, it couldn't hope to inflict a lethal wound.

(Then first‐I'll expose its core!)

Lux slipped through the countless branches flying about and approached the main body that was the trunk.

At the same time, the right arm of the Drag-Ride that was holding a large sword began to make a strange sound.

It was a gyrating sound of creaking metal. In order to block Lux's path, several branches formed a defensive wall that looked like a spider's wed. Then a single flash exploded out.

Recoil Burst.

It was the hidden technique that used both body control operation and mind control operation, by controlling them in opposite to each other instead of harmonizing them, it caused an intentional rampage.

The single attack that obtained the might of several dozen times a normal slash had broke apart countless branches, and gouged a large scar on the trunk.

(Did I do it? But, not yet‐)

Although the giant tree was shaved, but it didn't reach so far that its core was exposed.

The burden from using Recoil Burst was great, but he could only gamble here.

Lux didn't let the chance to win escape and launched the finishing attack.

He swung his large sword, erased the opening that should have resulted when his action ended, and persisted to shower the enemy with rain of slashes one after another without pause.

Infinitely continuing consecutive attack, End Action(Perpetual Links).

He shook off the burden and fatigue that was gradually piling up in him and attempted to make his blade reached the core, it was then,

*GAKIN-!*

Such metallic sound echoed. Yggdrasil repelled the blade of the large sword he swung down.

"Wha‐!?"

The moment the slash that he was about to unleash was stopped, Lux got hit consecutively by whip of branch and got blown away.

"Why!? Even though it shouldn't have been given time to even regenerate‐"

Celis yelled from behind.Hayes laughed loudly to that.

"Idiot! You thought that Yggdrasil will croak just from a few hundred of slash!? This monster can evolve even while getting attacked! With this, your specialty hidden techniques whatever are all used up!"

matter how much you bluff and enumerate your ideal, in the end you cannot save anything. HAHAHAHAHAHA!"

Part 6

Lux was inside the darkness.

His surrounding was covered with countless dark red branches. His DragRide was slowly constricted to smash it.

Yggdrasil was already surpassing the full power of Bahamut.

A sudden fatigue assaulted his whole body, it felt like his blood had become like mud.

'Someone who wasn't loved by anyone, will try to be loved ny anyone.'

It was true.

Lux thought that something like Black Hero was just a terrible irony.

He feared, and feared.

He tried to fight that mighty empire.

He tried to accomplish his duty as a prince.

He was putting on so much effort that his body might break apart.

"That's, not it."

Inside the sleepiness where he didn't understand if he was even awake or living.

Ride's limit! Use it! The Over Limit!'

No, that's not it.

The release code that Lisha sent to him.

He certainly remembered, that release method.

His thought ran off by its own and overtook his self from the past up to the present.

If he remembered right, this was‐.

'Lux! What's wrong!? That's, what in the world‐'

When he woke up in response to Lisha's yell, light was floating at Bahamut's surrounding.

All the code for the safety measure and output restriction emerged and warning signals were displayed one after another.

Originally, the utmost concentration in addition of training for the sake to remember the complicated procedure was needed to run the release code.

He had already seen several times the release procedure where this should be his first time doing it.

Before La Cruche used the procedure of full release that ignored the burden limit because the user Drag-Knight was puppet. Now Lux carried out the steps of that same procedure in high speed.

The mechanism of ability restriction that was used to protect the Drag-

Knight, he released them all until the last one without leaving a single one.

While La Cruche raised a shocked voice, even more letters and graphics made of light were unfolding.

They increased in number with accelerating speed, and the moment all the enumeration vanished, the suspended Bahamut activated.

Hayes's expression twitched and her eyes snapped wide open.

That instant, light flashed and along with it, the branches covering Lux burst out and a transformation started.

"Over Limit ‐ On"

Right after Lux whispered, light particles gathered at the surrounding in high speed, and additional summon was executed on the armor that was emitting ominous luster.

In the blink of eye, new pair of wings and various parts connected and the shape of huge dragon changed.

Both arms were attached with cartridge that was for high output flying mechanism and increasing the offense of the blade.

The dragon figure that expressed majesty uncovered its tyrannical true nature and accomplished transformation into a fiendish form that was specialized for offense.

Yggdrasil roared as though responding to the appearance of a formidable enemy and attacked.

Jet black slash line that split the space vertically instantly severed all those.

Hayes reflexively frowned seeing that hard to believe sight, it was then‐,

It wasn't a threat or even recommendation to surrender.

At the same time Bahamut was clad in flickering light that looked like flame and flew.

It created branches with hammer-like tips to crush the enemy.

Devilish branches were set forth, covering the whole field of vision.

The jet black streak ran every which way, dodging and cutting everything.

The full strength of Yggdrasil that had grown until it surpassed even Divine Drag-Ride was being completely excelled by Lux and Bahamut.

But‐,

The giant flesh tree that had its branches severed and its trunk pierced many times was starting to react gradually.

It doesn't have the power to finish with one blow my Yggdrasil‐the monster that has eaten several hundred Abysses. Thanks a lot false prince. For making my Yggdrasil‐into the strongest."

Something like a method to defeat the Ragnarok before them, it existed ‐nowhere.

Yggdrasil's trunk creaked at the same time with Hayes's bellow and the skull at the center opened its mouth gaping wide.

Yggdrasil's horn‐the tip that was generating shockwave hit Lux's large sword.

Impact that was incomparable with everything from before burst out and Lux's body should be blown away‐but.

*BIKIiiiII-!*

The created cracks increased in size and number with accelerating speed and the trunk was smashed up into pieces.

The special move that seized the starting point of enemy's attack, and then countered by returning back that attack strength as it was‐Critical Hit.

Even the performance of Reload on Fire that was a Divine Raiment of compression reinforcement, because of Over Limit, it was strengthened to the degree that it was able to amplify an attack's original might until nearly a hundred times.

The attack power of the Ragnarok that Lux raised up until now, and even the Over Limit at the end, everything was the groundwork for this.

For the sake of destroying the strongest Abyss that no one could win against using its own strength‐.

No matter what, something like a person who doesn't fear an enemy that is getting stronger endlessly‐something like a person who doesn't hold any fear whatsoever in planning to actually make use of that strength to strike back at such enemy, there is no way such person exist. Except this terrifying weakest enemy in front of you."

Ragnarok."

Fugil saw through that.

Epilogue: Promise

"So, you hid the Limit Break [Over Limit] from me again, how are you going to explain this? My dear brother."

"Well….."

In the academy's infirmary, the smell of drugs and decorative flowers in the room created an indescribably subtle atmosphere.

With his entire body wrapped in bandages, unable to move, Lux was being scolded by his sister Airi.

--It had been a week since they came back from Lies island. Lux had returned to the academy with everyone.

After that, Lux had no memory about escaping from the "Ark".

Due to the side effect of Limit Break [Over Limit], causing extreme fatigue and physical burden, he was unconscious for a full three days.

Waking up to see Airi with moist eyes made Lux reflect on his actions.

But now she was very calm, grumbling and complaining at Lux.

The [Ark] had vanished, no one knew its location.

The automatic doll Ra Kruse also disappeared inside the [Ark].

The New Kingdom had formed a blockage on all sea routes to investigate the [Ark], but due to the [Ark] characteristics of moving at sea, the search had proven itself to be difficult.

Relie was summoned to the Queen right after the event, but the punishment had yet to pass, for now she was detained with a serious warning.

Presumably in order to avoid problem in the next international event organized by the school ‐ the [Dragon War] where foreign countries would gather, measures were being taken to prevent chaos.

Right now --

"Airi-chan."

Suddenly a small voice was heard.

Lying on the bed next to Lux's, Philuffy supported herself up.

"Reprimanding on poor him, again?"

"…….u"

Being stared by that innocent eyes, Airi faltered in confusion.

How thoughtful, it was well known that Airi was not good at conveying feeling directly, unlike the frank Philuffy.

"Come, compare to these, soon it would be time for the School War and the Founding of New Kingdom memorial, we shouldn't be too conspicuous

--"

The Founding of New Kingdom memorial was held in the summer months after the demise of the Old Empire.

The revolution and the memorial were next to each other, although they were determined to go to the capital, Lux was the sinner of the Old Empire and would find it difficult to walk around in broad daylight.

Airi must had felt uneasy.

"On that matter--I decided to accept the good will of Lisha-sama."

"Eh……?"

Lux's statement made Airi froze in place.

"Because I was asked and she also wanted me to be her knight too--"

"Wait a minute!? What happened!? We cannot stand out, I told you that till my mouth was sour!?"

"Well, I understand what Airi wants to say……."

Looked at Lux smiling wryly, Airi stood up.

"That's not a problem. To become the exclusive knight of Lisha-sama

means--"

"Yes. I understand. It's just that--"

Staring at the dissatisfied Airi, Lux honestly explained.

"Because I think that is something I can do."

"Haa…. As expect my brother is my brother after all"

Airi suddenly lowered her shoulders feebly, sighing and muttered.

"I've got to go. There are ancient documents just found in the management room area, I would like to look at them a bit."

"We, also will be busy. Celes-senpai's parent--the Four Great Nobles family Ralgris seems to have something to discuss with me." "Please refuse them firmly."

Airi smiled and went away.

After the door closed, the room suddenly returned to its calm.

Philuffy, who ate a fruit silently next to him, glanced at Lux.

"The chest wound, has it healed?"

With only two people, Lux asked about the Abyss [Ragnarok] parasite-- Asked about Ratatosk.

The main source Yggdrasill had been eliminated, it seemed she would no longer be controlled.

"Yes. As long as I don't force myself there is no problem. And also, after getting used to the flute I can resist it, there is always a way."

Repeated use of the flute on the same Abyss would cause the body to have a certain degree of resistance.

And if she had a half human body, as long as she did not stop training, there would be no need to worry about being manipulated.

However, this was after all coming from a normal academy, Relie who had the full-detailed information of this, did not convey the matter to the New Kingdom. However, even so--

"Really,-- That's good."

"…….."

Lux hung his head in tears. Philuffy slowly rose up from her bed, went over in her pajama.

"You becomes a knight of Her Royal Highness, is that true?"

Philuffy inquired with the usual serious expression.

"Yes……they've also sent a letter to others during my absence.The officials in the Capital praised my achievements and intend to hand out a award-- this is what I think I want to do"

"…….."

"Although it would take time for the Capital and the local nobles to accept it, I cannot escape the crisis of the new kingdom. Moreover --"

"For me?"

"E--?"

"I was exposed as an [Abyss], so to make them silent, right?"

"………"

She found out.

She always expressed nothing at all, usually looked like an airhead. "When Lu-chan worries about things, you'll immediate be expose."

As a result, he had been seen through by his childhood friend.

"Sorry, at that time, I didn't protect you--"

He hung his head and spit out the words

"But, this time I will absolutely protect you!I promise you that time! I will create a peaceful country for Airi and Philuffy to live a happy life--E?"

A floating, sweet scent itched in his nasal, and then a soft feeling bloomed in him.

Philuffy, sitting next to Lux, clung tightly to Lux.

"Phi…..chan?"

"I, am fine."

Philuffy exposed a gentle smile she only showed to those she was closed with and softly whispered.

"Lu-chan is already protecting that promise?"

"E…….?

"My home, is right here. Because Lu-chan has done a good job creating one for me."

"……."

"Thank you, Lu-chan. I very, like you." Philuffy gently embraced Lux, who could not speak.

During that warm time.

Something had changed, Lux had found something precious.

Commissioned Short Story ‐ Secret Sleepover Meeting With The Girls

Part 1

"Then everybody, for those who will be able to stay over at Cross Field's first block, I want to ask them to stay the night there tomorrow. Applicants have the time to raise their hand until after school."

Those words that were suddenly announced caused the inside of the classroom to be stirred early in the morning.

The Academy that existed in the first block of Cross Field.

There was an assault by a mysterious force several days ago and a fierce battle unfolded in the campus.

Due to the great effort of the Drag-Knights including Lux, that danger was safely overcame but‐.

"Just as you know, due to the aforementioned incident, the school building and girl dormitory were damaged. They had been repaired as much as possible. But the repair for a part of them is still not finished. The rooms of the girl dormitory are especially problematic, several people are even unable to sleep there in this situation. Therefore, the number of hands for the repair will be increased again for the whole day tomorrow."

Here Raigree paused talking for a moment and looked around everyone in the class.

"But, during that time it will be a hindrance if there are people inside their room at that time. Thus, I'm taking application for volunteer to stay outside as a special case. The empty rooms will be used by students that cannot stay outside. Is there any question?"

The instructor's explanation finished and the class began.

By the way, there were sixteen students who wished to stay outside. It was a number for eight room in total.

(Staying outside, is it……. If possible it will be better for me to also stay outside though……)

Lux was thinking while doing his chore after school‐the cleaning up of the garden near girl dormitory.

The girls who were attending this academy for cultivating Drag-Knight were mostly young lady of noble family.

Although Cross Field's public order was relatively good, some rascal or bandit would sometime appear.

Surely it would be scary for them to have sleepover outside the Academy.

"However, me staying outside huh……"

He had experience sleeping out in the open air during his five years of livelihood doing chores, but as expected in his current position doing that would be problematic.

If possible he wanted to raise his hand for the sake of the other girls, but staying outside would need money.

He had a status as criminal in the new kingdom, and due to that he was burdened with debt that was a fraction of the national budget. He had no spare money.

Even now he was paying for his school expense and food expense by borrowing from Relie.

Normally he was doing chores, so he believed that there was no need for him to be really concerned about that but,

(If I told Airi, it feels like she will laugh at me again, saying that's really not fitting for a former prince……)

He suddenly thought such thing and smiled wryly, then,

"My? So you are in this kind of place. I was looking for you Lux-kun." Suddenly the voice of a grown up female came from behind Lux.

Relie Aingram.

She was the headmaster of the Academy and the successor of a great conglomerate. She was also an old acquaintance of Lux.

"Is it a request? For today there is still two more works, so if it's after that then‐"

"You are not wrong with the point that I want it done for the last, but this is not chore work. I wonder, do you know about the case of the girl dormitory's repair already?"

"Yes. I heard at the classroom this morning but, don't tell me‐?"

When Lux somehow got an idea and said that, Relie showed him a meaningful smile.

"Yes. As the headmaster, I'm also thinking a bit about that case. If possible, I want Lux-kun to also cooperate with the staying outside."

That matter itself was something that Lux actually wished to participate himself, but,

"I don't mind but, if it's an inn that is too expensive, my money won't‐"

Relie's sense of money couldn't possibly be measured by Lux who was used to a poor life.

When he was thinking about the price of a normal inn, it was possible that he wouldn't be able to pay with the money that he had in hand.

"Aah, you don't need to worry about that. It will be free."

Lux was perplexed hearing what Relie told him nonchalantly.

"Free, you said……"

Putting the burden on Relie was also something that would make him reluctant.

"Hm? It's an inn that I built, so there is no problem. The building itself is completed, but it's still not opened yet. That's why it's free. You get it?"

"……Ah, I understand."

He understood that the common sense he was thinking with was in a different dimension from hers.

When Lux answered like that in discomposure while sweating,

"Then, the contract is established. If you can possibly report to me later about the comfortableness of staying there, it will be helpful."

Relie made a smile and then left jauntily.

"Will it be okay……"

A place that was too high class would make him nervous though.

Lux who was feeling a tinge of anxiety resumed his chore and passed the day.

Part 2

And then, after the school the next day‐, at evening when the surrounding was dyed with madder red color.

Lux followed the route written in the map that Relie gave him and visited the inn at the first block.

"Is it fine here?"

In the center of a trade and amusement district that was conspicuously bustling even amidst the first block, a large building was standing.

The stone building that was equipped with a chimney might be provided with a large public bath at minimum.

Its appearance was the very definition of a high class inn for noble, from its wood material, the luster of the brick, and the design, it seemed like it took a lot of money to build it.

When Lux rang out the bell in front of the large door, the door was opened from inside.

"Welcome, please enter inside."

A butler clad in dress suit welcomed Lux inside while greeting him.

Next a maid who served as the reception came to him.

He heard that it still hadn't opened officially, but it seemed that it already had staffs.

Lux was slightly perplexed in this situation where he was inexperienced with, then,

"I will carry your baggage until the room, Lux Arcadia-sama."

"Ah, that's all right. I can carry it myself so‐"

Lux tried to refuse like that at the suggestion a maid girl wearing white prim, but,

"No. I'm grateful for your consideration, but I judged that it's unnecessary to act reserved. This is my role after all."

"I……see, then please‐wait, why is Noct here!?"

Lux reflexively raised his voice loudly when he noticed that fact.

The maid girl before him was a member of the famous trio in the Academy‐the Triad.

"……Nii-san, please don't be so loud. It makes my concentration broke in the middle of my reading."

"Even Airi is here!? Why in the world‐!?"

Seeing his little sister addressing him from the second floor's atrium, Lux raised a bewildered voice once more.

"It's not just missy Airi here, Lux-kun."

"You're finally here eh, Lux-chi. Everyone is already gathered y'know"

Looking carefully, he noticed that the staff in butler outfit just now was one of the Triad, Sharis.

And then even Tillfur in her uniform appeared beside Airi.

"Why, everyone of the Triad is‐?"

Airi and the Triad approached beside Lux who was dumbfounded.

"However, personally I'm a bit shocked. You were completely tricked thinking me as a male staff. Even like this I have quite the size for breast though. ‐I'm really hurt, young man."

"Ah, I, I'm sorry."

When Lux who was poked by Sharis who dressed like a male became flustered, she smiled wryly saying "It's a joke".

"Yes. However, I judged that Sharis simply reap what she sow. In the first place, it was you who planned 'this' after all."

"Eh……!? That's, you mean……"

A bad premonition came inside Lux.

Certainly this morning Airi talked to him about staying outside, but,

"I'll say this beforehand, I'm pretty much opposing this you know? I thought that perhaps I should let Nii-san to relax alone in a place without girl sometimes, but……"

"……Ah, it's Lu-chan."

At that moment, the door inside opened and another girl showed up.

The familiar pink hair and expressionlessly absentminded face were definitely the feature of his childhood friend Philuffy.

She was wearing casual clothes that he had never really seen in

Academy‐a pure white blouse, and chic black skirt with short length. In a glance it was a combination of subdued color, but it emphasized the presence of her large breasts and Lux's gaze was naturally nailed to it.

"Eh, Philuffy also came here?"

The entrance of his hidden roommate caused Lux to be even more confused.

If he remembered correctly, Philuffy didn't say anything about staying outside at this morning but‐,

"Just before this, Onee-chan told me, to stay in this inn."

"…………"

His thinking was naïve.

There was no way Relie who was doting to her little sister wouldn't arrange this kind of 'coincidence'.

She was hiding the truth until just before, trying to make Lux and Philuffy to stay in the same inn.

(Even though we have been staying in the same room already every day, she doesn't need to do something like this too‐)

Lux was bewildered while noticing something out of place.

"But……, for Airi to be here too‐?"

"This is the so called beautiful sibling love y'know, Lux-chi."

In respond to Tillfur's words, Airi cleared her throat *cough* and cut in.

"When I heard from Nii-san about you staying outside, I questioned the headmaster and made her talk. There was no way I can let Nii-san to stay outside with only Philuffy-san, so I suggested that I along with the Triad will also stay here. And then Sharis-senpai thought about surprising Nii-san‐"

"…………"

He understood the full picture with that one sentence.

Lux was somewhat nervous about staying at the inn that was affiliated with Aingram conglomerate, but he was a bit relieved inside his heart seeing that everyone here was his acquaintance.

(No but wait a second……. In the end the fact that I'm the only man here doesn't change though‐?)

Wasn't it something he should be even more nervous about……?

"Well, in any case, let's cooperate with each other to pass through this night! By the way Lux-kun. I want to ask you to go shopping for the dinner though, will you do it?"

"Ah, yes. I'll go."

Lux nodded at Sharis's request and everyone entrusted money to him, then he went outside.

Part 3

"Even so, it become something difficult huh……"

He picked up food with somewhat larger quantity and good quality as much as possible.

If it was just him alone, then he would be able to finish this with just cheap and simple dish, but as expected he would have to be considerate with several other girls also staying there with him.

Lux was in charge of shopping for food was because there was mostly no girl who had ever gone shopping for food ingredient in the city. And with Lux alone, he also wouldn't be standing out. Those were Airi's thinking.

"Certainly it's better to not stand out, but I wish at least one girl will come along with me."

"My? Why is that I wonder?"

"As expected, I don't understand what kind of food a girl will like, I'm confused what will everyone like to eat."

"I think you don't need to be thinking that hard you know? But, if the number of people is quite many, then it will be desirable to have some variation of the food. I believe what is necessary to be put inside that basket will be some fruit for dessert."

"Ah, you're right. As expected from Krulcifer-san. ‐Since when you are there!?"

Lux finally noticed the girl beside him after talking quite much and yelled so.

"You were talking along with me really well there, so I thought you had noticed right from the beginning."

The girl with bluish white long hair and beautiful look that was fairy-like said that while brushing up her hair coolly.

"Why is Krulcifer-san in this kind of place‐?"

"It's a coincidence I think?"

"…………"

Lux couldn't say anything in front of the smile with deep meaning of this overseas student.

"If I have to expose the trick, it's because I have a bit of business with you. You see, it seems that a reservation for two can be made in a nearby inn."

"That's, could it be……?"

"Yes. If you like, I'm thinking to invite you there. But‐as expected this is too sudden and I got beaten to the punch. It was careless of me."

"……Sorry. That, it might be impossible if Krulcifer-san had already put a reservation there but, if you like, then Krulcifer-san can also stay over‐"

"Thank you. I was waiting for that word."

Krulcifer chuckled slightly and stood at his side.

"Then, seeing that we have two people here for carrying things, let's continue the shopping for a bit more. Lux-kun want at least a girl to accompany you right?"

"Ah, yes."

When he noticed, he had already got carried by Krulcifer's pace.

Even when her plan crumbled, she immediately corrected her course flawlessly. Lux thought that it was really like her.

After that, they shopped for a while before Lux and Krulcifer returned to the inn‐.

"You are slow Lux! How long you are planning to make me wait!"

"Why even Lisha-sama is coming here!?"

When he opened the door, the petite girl who was the princess of the new kingdom was standing there with folded arms, wearing uniform and a white gown above it.

"A, about that……. The Drag-Ride atelier can be used for sleepover, so I was thinking to have you accompany me there for a bit and so I went looking for you……. No wait, why is Krulcifer beside you huh!?"

"I only met him by chance because our shopping destination was the same. More importantly, surely you were trying to have sleepover together with him in your own way, but as expected, I think it's questionable to make other person to sleep in that atelier……"

"Wha-……!?"

When Krulcifer pointed that out with a really doubtful expression, Lisha's face went red and she got flustered, then,

"My stomach is empty, let's make dinner soon, okay?"

Philuffy in her casual clothes interrupted with an indifferent face and stopped the two.

As expected, Philuffy who was always in her own pace was strong in this kind of time.

Lux thought of such thing. After that he was going to use the kitchen of the inn and cooked for everyone.

"Fuh, the prince can just take rest for a bit. To tell you the truth‐we've got nothing to do until now!"

"Yep yep! I thought I was going to die from feeling too bored!"

"No. I think you who didn't help with the bed making have no right to say that, Tillfur."

Each of the three members of Triad said that and took on the cooking duty.

Lux followed what he was told and took a break at the entrance. By the time the nice smell of cooking was drifting‐.

*Knock knock*. The sound of light knocking could be heard.

"Who is it? At this kind of time‐"

Airi who was sitting on the chair in front of him tilted her head and murmured.

It was indeed strange. This inn still hadn't been opened formally, and there should be no signboard put up yet, and yet.

"Excuse me. I, is there an empty room in this inn that can be used? That's, it will help if I can stay just for one night if possible."

While they were thinking that, the voice of a young girl unexpectedly came saying that.

However, as expected there was no way they could make arbitrary decision to allow a normal customer to stay.

"No. This inn is still not opened."

"Ple, please. It might be a bother for this to be so sudden but, today there is nowhere I can go‐"

"Eh……?"

Lux noticed something in the middle of conversation.

The voice and tone felt familiar somehow to him. Thinking that it wasn't possible, he opened the door. There‐.

"Even Celis-senpai!? Why are you in this kind of place‐"

The appearance of the very unexpected person caused Lux to yell unconsciously.

"Lu, Lux!? Why are you here‐!? Is this where you are having sleepover outside!?"

Both sides were surprised, so first Lux explained about the situation.

After that, he also asked Celis about her circumstance. Then she averted her face looking as though it was really hard for her to say.

"Eerr, about that……. A junior of mine planned to stay outside, but suddenly she became unable and was troubled. That girl isn't really knowledgeable about Cross Field, so I accepted to take her place in staying outside and went out but‐. When I went to look, the inn where I planned to stay had gone bankrupt……"

Celis hung her head down, her shoulders dropped dejectedly.

"Err, if Celis-senpai doesn't mind, you can stay together with us here."

"I'm in your debt Lux! I will repay this favor back without fail!"

Seeing Celis's sparkling eyes, Lux smiled wryly while calling out to everyone.

In the end, the dishes that were made from the ingredients that he bought a lot of were settled inside everyone's stomach without any leftover.

After that everyone chatted with each other before the time for sleeping arrived, but then‐.

"This is troubling. ‐To think that there is not enough beds."

"I had somehow thought that this will be the case……"

Krulcifer's murmur was responded by Airi with a really complicated face.

Although the inn still wasn't open, but there was some rooms that could be used, and yet because the number of people increased too many, the beds weren't enough.

Furthermore they could only prepare a big room for use of group customer. Everyone had to sleep in the same room.

"What's more, we only lack one bed coincidentally……. So, what to do now?"

No one replied back to Lisha's muttering.

But, Philuffy who had changed into negligee entered into a bed the very fist and,

"It's fine. It's a bit cramped but, Lu-chan can also enter here you know?"

She rubbed her eyes sleepily while saying that. At that moment, the surrounding became noisy.

"Oi wait! What are you saying this airheaded girl! As expected that will be

ba‐"

"Uwaa!? I think I still haven't finished my heart's preparation……"

Lisha and Tillfur started to make noise, and Lux was also flustered.

When Celis who saw that tried to calm them down, Krulcifer smiled coolly.

"That's quite a good idea. Then, how about everyone sleep on the bed, and if Lux-kun come asking, then it will be by each one's own judgment whether to lend a space or not. How about that?"

"Eeeeh!?"

Just when he thought the situation would surely be settled, Lux became even more flustered with Krulcifer's suggestion.

"Please wait! I won't allow such indecent act! Sleeping together is only for those below ten years old, that is the precept of my Ralgris house‐"

"Oh? Celis, could it be, if Lux-kun ask if he could borrow a sleeping space, will you plan to do something indecent? Well, he is also a man, it's not unreasonable to be unable to trust him but‐"

(I think that's not the problem……!)

When Lux was going to retort at Sharis's statement‐,

"I, I absolutely won't do anything like that. Be, besides I believe in Lux‐I understand. Please come to my bed anytime you like!"

"No, that's no good you know!? How does it become like that!?"

Celis became triggered by Sharis's provocation and in the end even the person of common sense Celis became flustered.

"Then, then I too will……. Tha, that is‐, it will be only half okay!" Lisha who saw that also entered the room timidly, then everyone followed.

In the end everyone entered the bed and turned off the light.

"……Haa. In a sense, this is relaxing I think."

After Lux was paralyzed for a while, he moved to the entrance.

And then, with a leftover blanket in hand, he slept on a large sofa.

"Good night, everyone."

Part 4

Inside the big room after Lux vanished, voices could be heard from the darkness.

"As expected, there is no sign he is coming to anyone's bed isn't it? I have expected it but‐"

"……You are going to say something like that despite having been expecting it, Krulcifer?"

"Yes, either way he will surely say that he will endure, so surely it will end without any fuss."

After answering like that to Lisha's voice, the night grew deeper along with the silence.

However the sleepover that should have ended without any incident was disturbed with a commotion that occurred the next morning.

Unnoticed, Philuffy was sleeping together with Lux at the entrance. According to her,

'When going back from the toilet, I was sleepy and mistook my own bed.' She said.
